Long Lasting Windscreen Protection

Q2 View has established an industry standard for window coating. Its durability made it the choice for advanced detailing enthusiasts and professionals. Q2 View EVO showcases its quality with simple application via Q2M GlassPolish, providing improved durability and resistance. It endures on the most frequently used windscreen for up to 24 months, preserving water repellency. The side windows can last for 36 months.

Q2 View's EVO enhances safety for drivers and passengers, improving comfort in challenging road conditions. Poorer road conditions require greater driver focus on driving. Q2 View EVO improves road visibility through clean windows, repelling water and dirt, and increasing transparency. Q2 View EVO enhances slickness, leading to reduced ice and snow adhesion.

In 2021, the company made progress by revamping its paint coating line-up, known as EVO. Two years later, they take pride in achieving similar successes with their other coatings. All EVO coatings provide ease of application, increased durability, and resistance, offering up to 50% more in everyday use.

Essential is surface preparation. Skipping Q2M GlassPolish is inadvisable, as it functions as a cleaner and bonding agent. Proper preparation is required for Q2 Repel EVO to achieve anticipated durability. The user prefers Q2M GlassPolish applied by machine using a Q2M Polish Pad, which works well at low revs. Once a light film of residue is present, it should be wiped off with Q2M Prep. Avoid overapplication. Q2 Repel EVO should be applied generously in a circular motion. Reapply the product to create a thicker layer, concentrating mainly on the windscreen. A damp cloth should be used to remove the residue.

- Hydrophobic barrier repels water & dirt
- Windows stay cleaner, longer
- Visibility during heavy rain significantly improved
- Ice & snow do not adhere so firmly making clearing easier
- Lasts up to 24 months

- Durability: >24 months / 50,000 km
- Self cleaning: 50 kp/h

- Alcohol tolerance: full

How To Use

- Apply Gyeon Q2 View EVO in a dry, shaded area.
- Preparation: Wash > decontaminate windows.
- Wet rayon applicator block with Gyeon Q2 Cleanse, work into windows using moderate pressure.
- Buff off residue with damp PB Utility Towel.
- Soak Gyeon Q2M Applicator Suedes with Gyeon Q2 Repel, work into windows.
- Buff off residue with dry PB Utility Towel.
- Leave car warm and dry for 12 hours to allow SiO2 coating to cure.
- Accelerate process by heating treated windows to 60 degrees C for 10 minutes.

We Say

Gyeon Q2 View EVO is a quartz coating system specifically formulated to make automotive glass water repellent. If, like us, you always question relative performance in the world of car care, then you're probably wondering how Gyeon Q2 View EVO differs to rival products, and what it offers that they don't? Well, for starters, Gyeon Q2 View EVO is supplied as a kit that includes both a cleaner (Gyeon Q2 Cleanse) and the coating itself (Gyeon Q2 Repel), along with the necessary applicators. This is not only convenient, but also offers excellent value for money compared to buying similar products separately from other brands. Moving on, the performance that Gyeon Q2 View offers is second to none. We've used it on several of our daily drivers in recent years, and it offers a number of other benefits in addition to vastly improving visibility in wet weather conditions. These include making it easier to wash off bug splatter and bird droppings, reducing the degree to which the windows freeze over during the winter months and making it much easier to defrost windows that have frozen over. The latter is most welcome on cold winter mornings when you just want to get in your car and be on your way! Finally, the durability offered by Gyeon Q2 View EVO is also very impressive, and the drop-off over time is slow and progressive. On our daily drivers, we usually reapply the system just once a year to maintain maximum performance.

Key Features

Beading: 10/10 (Compared To Others)
Durability: 24 Months+ (Average Value)
Runoff Threshold: 32 mph (When Glass Is Clean)

Description

Gyeon Q2 View EVO is an advanced quartz-based coating system that forms a semi-permanent hydrophobic (water-hating) barrier layer on automotive glass. It achieves this via two distinct products that are supplied as a kit; Gyeon Q2 Cleanse and Gyeon Q2 Repel. The former is a chemical polish and silica-rich bonding agent, while the latter is a hydrophobic glass coating containing functional silica- and fluorine-based components. When used systematically (which is strictly necessary in order to obtain maximum performance), these two products form a highly durable, fully transparent SiO2-based coating that vigorously repels water. As a result, rain drops and road spray simply bead up and roll off of treated surfaces, or are blown off when driving speeds rise above 30 mph. Gyeon Q2 View therefore significantly improves visibility in wet weather, and greatly reduces the need to use your windscreen wipers. The extreme beading also tends to pick up and carry away fresh dirt and grime, meaning that the coating is partially self-cleaning. Furthermore, in drier weather bug splatter washes off far more easily, and in colder weather defrosting is more quickly achieved. Gyeon Q2 View EVO is currently supplied as a pre-packed kit containing a 20 ml bottle of Gyeon Q2 Cleanse, a 20 ml bottle of Gyeon Q2 Repel, a rayon applicator block, a Gyeon Q2M Applicator Block, four Gyeon Q2M Applicator Suedes and an instruction booklet.

Specification

Adds Protection: Yes
Application Method: By hand only
Beading: 10
Chemical Basis: Silica-based (fluorinated)
Dangerous Goods: Y
Durability: 24 months+
Emits Strong Fumes: Yes
Layerable: No
Runoff Threshold: 30 mph
Safe For Privacy Glass: Yes
Safe For Window Tints: No
Size: 20 ml Kit
Slickness: 10

How To Use

You should apply Gyeon Q2 View EVO in a dry place out of direct sunlight. In all cases, prepare the windows you are going to treat in the normal way (wash > decontaminate). Next, lightly wet the supplied rayon applicator block with Gyeon Q2 Cleanse and work it into the surface of the windows in a circular fashion, using moderate pressure and tight overlapping strokes. Once all of the windows are treated, go back around the car buffing off the residue with a damp PB Utility Towel until a smear-free finish is achieved. Next, soak one of the supplied Gyeon Q2M Applicator Suedes with Gyeon Q2 Repel, wrap it around the supplied Gyeon Q2M Applicator Block and work it into the surface of the windows in a circular fashion, using moderate pressure and tight overlapping strokes; you will need to re-wet the suede applicator with product before treating each window, as Gyeon Q2 Repel flashes off quite quickly. Once all of the windows are treated, go back around the car buffing off the residue with a dry PB Utility Towel until a perfect smear-free finish is achieved. The car must then be left somewhere warm and dry for a minimum of 12 hours to allow the SiO2 coating to cure fully (if you wish, you can accelerate this process by heating the treated windows to 60 degrees C for 10 minutes using an infra-red heat lamp).

Long lasting protection for glass!

Gyeon Q2 View is a long-lasting coating that helps glass repel water, dust, dirt, snow, and other environmental contaminants. This unique formula provides crystal clear protection and is extremely hydrophobic, so each drop of water that hits your windshield will bead up and roll off taking any dirt or dust nearby with it. Gyeon Q2 View can be used on any exterior glass including the windshield, side glass, and mirrors, and it lasts up to 12 months!

When you're on the road one thing is for sure: you need to be able to see the road ahead. While glass cleaner may take care of smudges and fingerprints, it won't do anything when you're driving down the highway in a rainstorm! Windshield wipers help, but tend to simply smear things around. Gyeon Q2 View on the other hand actively helps control the amount of rain and soil that remains on your windshield and exterior glass.

Gyeon Q2 View repels rain, snow, sleet, dust, dirt, and other contaminants for an entire year with just one application. Gyeon Q2 View will even cut down on windshield wiper use, prolonging the life of your wiper blades! The extremely hydrophobic formula allows any moisture to roll away, even when the weather gets rough. Since water won't be smeared all over the windshield, your field of vision will be more crisp and even at night, you'll have a much better view of the road ahead.

Directions:

Always work on clean, dry glass. Clean glass with a high quality glass cleaner prior to application.

- Use a thick applicator sponge to apply GYEON Q2 Cleanse in a circular pattern
- Wipe away any residue with a clean, damp cloth. Allow surface to dry completely.
- Using the included applicator, apply GYEON Q2 Repel using circular motions.
- Allow to set for a few minutes, then polish lightly with a clean microfiber cloth.
- Allow product to cure for a few hours prior to exposure to water.

INNOVACAR SC3’ÜN FAYDALARI | Gelişmiş Görüş, Su ve Kir Tutmayan Cam Koruması

INNOVACAR SC3 GLASS SEALANT, otomobil camlarında yağmur, kireç, yağ ve yol kirlerine karşı dirençli koruyucu bir film oluşturan nanoteknolojik cam kaplama ürünüdür. Gelişmiş su itici (hidrofobik) etkisi sayesinde, 50 km/s gibi düşük hızlarda bile camdan suyun hızla akmasını sağlayarak görüşü artırır ve güvenli sürüş sağlar.
• Su ve Yağ İtici Etki: Cam üzerinde boncuklanma (beading) ve tabakalaşma (sheeting) etkisi oluşturur.
• Kireç ve Kir Önleyici: Cam yüzeyde oluşabilecek kireç ve toz birikimini geciktirir.
• Silecek Uyumlu Formül: Moleküler seviyede oluşturduğu kaplama sürtünmeye neden olmaz.

SC3 NASIL KULLANILIR? | Uygulama Talimatları

1. Hazırlık:
o Cam yüzey DS SCALE ile dekontamine edilmeli, gerekiyorsa kil bar kullanılmalıdır.
o Cila ve wax kalıntıları varsa D2 CHECK ile yüzey temizlenmelidir.

2. Uygulama:
o Ürünü kuru ve gölge bir alanda uygulayın.
o SC3’ü Micron Suede beze damlatın ve yüzeye önce dikey, sonra yatay hareketlerle uygulayın.
o Yaklaşık 1 dakika bekleyin, ardından temiz ve kuru bir mikrofiber bezle yüzeyi silin.

3. İsteğe Bağlı 2. Katman:
o Etkiyi artırmak için 20 dakika sonra ikinci katman uygulanabilir.

4. Aktivasyon Süreci:
o Ürün 7 saat içinde tam olarak aktifleşir.
o Bu süre zarfında yağmur, kar, yıkama gibi dış etkenlerden koruyun.

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Cam yüzeyi DS SCALE ile dekontamine edin, gerekiyorsa kil bar kullanın.
2. Cila ve wax kalıntıları varsa D2 CHECK ile yüzeyi temizleyin.
3. Kuru ve gölge alanda SC3'ü Micron Suede beze damlatın.
4. Önce dikey, sonra yatay hareketlerle yüzeye uygulayın.
5. Yaklaşık 1 dakika bekleyin, temiz mikrofiber bezle silin.
6. 20 dakika sonra ikinci katman uygulanabilir (isteğe bağlı).
7. Ürün 7 saat içinde tam aktifleşir; bu sürede yağmur, kar, yıkamadan koruyun.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Cam yüzeylerde yağmur, kireç, yağ ve yol kirlerine karşı hidrofobik koruma için kullanılır. Evde duş kabini ve balkon camlarında da kullanılabilir.

### Detaylı Açıklama
Modern boyayı koruma filmlerine (PPF), vinil kaplamalara ve wrap’lere özel formüle edilen Q² PPF EVO, tek kat uygulamada mükemmel hidrofobi, UV kalkanı ve ipeksi kayganlık kazandıran esnek bir SiO² kaplamadır. EVO güncellemesiyle kimyasal direncini ve ömrünü P’ye varan oranda artırır; parlak ya da mat fark etmeksizin film yüzeyini daha kolay temizlenir hâle getirir.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

•	Esnek Tek Kat – Kaplamalı & self-healing tüm PPF/vinil türlerine tam uyum
•	24 Ay / 30 000 km Koruma – pH 2-11 kimyasallara karşı yüksek direnç
•	Üst Düzey Hidrofobi – 110 °+ temas açısı, güçlü self-cleaning etkisi
•	Renk Canlandırıcı – Parlak filmde derinlik, mat filmde eşit satensi korur
•	Ekonomi + Hız – 30 ml şişe ? 50 ml eski versiyon; hızlı uygulama aplikatörü dahildir

Nasıl Uygulanır?

1.	Hazırlık
o	Aracı yıka › demir/tar arındır › yıka › durula › kurula.
o	Film Canlandırma (isteğe bağlı) – Q²M PPF Renew ile mikro-çizik giderme & parlaklık/saten tazeleme.
o	 Son Yağ Alma – Tüm yüzeyi Q²M Prep veya Q²M DegreaseTabs solüsyonu ile panel panel silin; hav bırakmayan mikrofiber kullanın..
2.	Ekipmanı Hazırla
o	Kutudan çıkan Coating Applicator Mini’yi alın, yeni süetle sarın.
o	Şişeyi çalkalayın, süete 6-8 damla damlatın.
3.	Criss-Cross Uygulama
o	Omuz genişliğinde panel seçin.
o	Dikey › yatay geçişlerle ince, homogren film oluşturun.
o	Parlak veya mat fark etmez; ürünü “ıslak, eşit” görünümde bırakın.
4.	Terleme & Silme Zamanı
o	20-40 sn içinde “terleme” (hafif boncuk/sis) başlar.
o	1. bez: Q²M BaldWipe ile kalıntıyı nazikçe al.
o	2. bez: Q²M SoftWipe ile yüzeyi parlat / sateni eşitle.
o	Spot ışığıyla kontrol et, iz kalırsa hemen düzelt.
5.	Kürleşme
o	Araç 12 saat kuru, tozsuz ortamda beklesin; 24 saat su görmemeli.
o	IR lamba (60 °C × 10 dk) ile süreyi kısaltabilirsiniz.
o	İlk 7 gün deterjan kullanmayın; sadece saf su ile durulayın.
6.	Bakım
o	Yıkamalarda Q²M PPF Wash şampuanı kullanın.
o	Hidrofobiyi tazelemek için 4-6 haftada bir Q²M PPF Maintain spreyi uygulayın.

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ)

Q: Mat PPF’de parlaklık yapar mı?
A: Hayır. Mat/satensi filmde görünümü değiştirmez; sadece yüzeyi eşit hidrofobik tabakayla kaplar.
Q: Tek kat yeterli mi?
A: Evet. Kaplama kalın formüldür; üretici 1 kat önerir. İkinci kat gerekmez.
Q: Kaplama film self-healing özelliğini bozar mı?
A: Hayır. Esnek polimer yapısı filmle birlikte hareket eder; self-healing performansı korunur.
Q: Dış mekânda uygulayabilir miyim?
A: Rüzgârsız, gölge ve 15-25 °C arası stabil koşullarda evet, ancak ilk 12 saat yağmur-toz temasından kaçınmalısınız.

Film korumasını bir üst seviyeye taşıyın: GYEON Q² PPF EVO ile uzun ömürlü hidrofobi, ipeksi kayganlık ve UV kalkanı tek katla aracınızda!

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Aracı yıkayın, PPF/vinil yüzeyi demir ve zift temizleyicilerle arındırın.
2. İsteğe bağlı olarak Q²M PPF Renew ile mikro-çizik giderme ve yüzey tazeleme yapın.
3. Tüm yüzeyi Q²M Prep ile panel panel silin, yağsız zemin oluşturun.
4. Coating Applicator Mini'yi süetle sarın, 6-8 damla damlatın.
5. Dikey ve yatay criss-cross geçişlerle ince, homojen film oluşturun.
6. 20-40 sn içinde terleme başladığında Q²M BaldWipe ile silin.
7. Araç 12 saat kuru ortamda beklesin; ilk 7 gün deterjan kullanmayın.

## Gloss, satin, matte films

Q² PPF EVO is a unique ceramic coating for Paint Protection Film. It is a very easy-to-apply, flexible, one-layer coating designed for all types of PPF and Vinyl, whether it be gloss, matte, or satin. The coating is formulated to enhance self-cleaning and maximize the hydrophobic properties of any automotive film while maintaining high durability. Will not affect modern PPF's self-healing capabilities.

PH TOLERANCE: 2-11
DURABILITY: up to 24 MONTHS

Product Images:
-
-
-

## Best Practices & Pro-Tips

Q² PPF EVO must be applied like a regular coating with a criss-cross motion. Ensure good preparation of the paint protection film using Q²M PPF RENEW, followed by Q²M PREP for optimal surface bonding.
TIP: Work with reflected light; it will make streaks or smudges more visible and help eliminate them over time. Use the Q²M Suede to perfect the finish.

## Description

### GYEON PPF EVO Ceramic Coating 50ml

#### Advanced quartz technology combined with user-friendly characteristics

MAJOR FEATURES:
- UNIQUE, NEW FLUORO-MODIFIED POLYSILAZANES TECHNOLOGY

Unique quartz coating for Paint Protection Film. Q² PPF is very easy to apply flexible one layer coating for all types of PPF & Vinyl. It is designed to extend self-cleaning and maximize hydrophobic properties of any automotive film while being highly durable.

BOX CONTAINS: Q² PPF EVO 50ML / APPLICATOR / 4 SUEDE CLOTHS
AVAILABLE CAPACITIES: 50 ML

## Best Practice and Pro-Tips from Yves Heylen

Q² PPF must be applied like a regular coating with criss-cross motion. Ensure good preparation of the paint protection film using Q²M PPF RENEW follow by Q²M PREP for optimal surface bonding. TIP: Work with reflected light. It will make streaks or smudges more visible and help eliminate them in time. Use the Q²M Suede to perfect the finish.

## Flexible One Layer Coating

Q² PPF has been designed to match & perform with all modern paint protection film structure & self-healing properties.

## Hard & Durable

The unique chemical structure of Q² PPF makes it the hardest coating for vinyl wrap & ppf on the market while being super slick & easy to apply. It will add great chemical resistance & hydrophobic properties to the surface, creating a thick & slick layer of protection without compromising the self-healing capabilities of the film it been applied to.

Q² PPF is a flexible, one layer ceramic coating designed to protect PPF and colour change wraps. The unique chemical composition of Q² PPF makes it super slick and easy to apply. It will add great chemical resistance and hydrophobic properties to the surface, creating a thick & slick layer of protection without compromising the self-healing capabilities of the film it been applied to.

Application possible on all types of PPF. On used films, we highly recommend to prepare the film with Q²M PPF Renew.

## Prevents yellowing

Q² PPF EVO has been designed to perform with all modern paint protection films, including coated and self-healing versions. It will enhance the color on both glossy and matte film without changing the finish. The unique composition of Q² PPF EVO, featuring fluoro-modified polysilazanes, makes it the most durable and hydrophobic coating for PPF available. It remains very slick and easy to apply. It can be applied on both glossy or matte film, as well as on any vinyl wrap surface. It creates a slick, protective layer without compromising the self-healing abilities of the film.

DURABILITY: 4/5
GLOSS: 6/6
BEADING: 5/5
SELF-CLEANING: 5/5

## Application

Considering you've already done all the necessary prep work, applying GYEON PPF EVO is very easy. Simply apply a few drops onto your applicator and work in a 2x2' criss-cross motion. Let it set for about ~2 minutes, then wipe off the excess with one microfiber and follow it up with another wipe using another clean towel. PPF EVO is designed to go onto grabby and porous film surfaces, making it very easy to remove. If you've used a paint coating on films before, you'll notice that films will absorb coatings at an uneven rate, making it difficult to buff off and will leave a haze.

### Outdoor-friendly application

All GYEON coatings can be applied outdoors. Ensure stable conditions, never use in direct sunlight and check the weather forecast! Cut down cure time to ~1 minute before wiping off.

### Gloss, Satin, Matte films compatible

PPF EVO will not 'add gloss' to a matte finish; it will enhance the color and the matte look, making it richer. It will do the same for satin films as well and works on colored vinyl wraps.

## GYEON PPF EVO FAQs

Q: How long does it last?
A: Around 2 years, or more if applied multiple layers and maintained well with PPF Wash and PPF Maintain.

Q: Does it add 'gloss' to matte or satin films?
A: No, but it will enhance the matte finish to a richer appearance, similar to applying lotion on dry hands. GYEON PPF EVO is fully matte film compatible.

Q: When do I wipe it off?
A: Simply apply a few drops onto your applicator and work in a 2x2' criss-cross motion. Let it set for about ~2 minutes, then wipe off the excess with one microfiber and follow it up with another wipe using another clean towel.

Q: What's the layering time?
A: Layering time is between 1 to 4 hours, and full curing occurs within 48 hours. You can take the vehicle out after 12 hours.

Q: How much will the bottle do?
A: You'll use slightly more product than regular paint coatings because you want to apply more for the film to absorb into it as well. For a mid-sized sedan, you'll use around ~25 ml per coat; the 50ml bottle will be sufficient for you to do 2 layers.

Q: After coating, when can I bring the vehicle out?
A: The vehicle can be driven the next day, or approximately 12 hours later. It is advisable to avoid exposing the coating to water within the first 24 hours.

Q: How cold (or hot) can I apply the coating under?
A: A temperature of at least 10°C is recommended, although you can still attempt the application between 5°C to 10°C if necessary. If the temperature reaches 30°C, then it's on the warmer side, and you will need to retreat into the shade.

Q: What do I maintain it with and how often?
A: Wash with GYEON PPF Wash; this is a decon-soap that is effective at removing contaminants without the need to use a clay bar (which can scratch your film). Top it with GYEON PPF Maintain to keep the water beading and prolong the coating's resistance to film yellowing.

Q: I have a 'high-spot', what do I do?
A: High spots refer to dried coatings that were not completely buffed off. If you catch the high spots within 30 minutes, you can use the coating itself again to level/soften the high spots. If it's been a few days, then you'll need to mechanically polish it off with PPF Renew and reapply coating on the affected area.

Q: What's the expiration date? New and opened.
A: Officially, Gyeon recommends the product to be used within 2 to 3 years when new. If the bottle has been opened, it's best to use up the product in 1 to 2 months to preserve the coating's maximum effectiveness.

Q: Can it be shipped in the cold?
A: No problem at all. Coatings contain a significant amount of solvents and exhibit high chemical stability.

Q: Anything else I should know?
A: Make sure to use a little more product than regular paint coatings because films are much more porous than paint. You want enough product to be absorbed into the porous film as well and not only sit on top. PPF EVO is a flexible coating that penetrates the film and will not affect the film's self-healing abilities. If your film already has a hydrophobic coating on it, it's encouraged for you to apply PPF EVO over it to prolong its OEM hydrophobic layer.

## Product Description

The Gyeon PPF Evo is an advanced ceramic coating that offers unrivaled protection and clarity for your vehicle's PPF (Paint Protection Film) surfaces! This protective coating is engineered with cutting-edge materials and formulation to provide an exceptional shield against the hazards of everyday driving. PPF Evo is designed to guard your vehicle's paintwork from swirls, scratches, road debris, bug stains, and other common sources of damage. What sets the Gyeon PPF Evo apart is the unique composition of fluoro modified polysilazanes, which makes it incredibly durable & hydrophobic. It remains very slick, easy to apply and it can be applied on both glossy or matte film but also on any vinyl wrap surface. It creates a slick, protective layer without compromising the self-healing abilities of the film. It will enhance color on both glossy and matte films without changing the finish as well. To apply, add a few drops of PPF Evo to your microfiber suede and work panel by panel with crisscross motions. Reflected light is key here as it will highlight streaks or smudges for quick removal, leaving behind a perfect surface. In addition to its exceptional protection and clarity, the Gyeon PPF Evo is also known for its long-lasting durability. Engineered to withstand the rigors of daily driving, this PPF boasts excellent resistance against UV rays, discoloration, and environmental contaminants. It maintains its integrity even in harsh weather conditions, ensuring your vehicle remains shielded and maintains its showroom-quality appearance. With proper care you can expect durability of up to 24 months! With its advanced technology, unbeatable clarity, and long-lasting durability, the Gyeon PPF Evo is a great option for your PPF protection needs!

1. Yüzeyin tamamen temiz ve kuru olduğundan emin olun.
2. Ürünü yüzeye 2–3 kez doğrudan püskürtün (yaklaşık 100–150 ml/m²).

5. Ürün 1 saat içinde kurur, tam etkinlik 7 saatte oluşur.
6. Sıcak yüzeylerde ve güneş altında uygulamaktan kaçının.

GYEON Q² Tire, dünyanın ilk SiO² içerikli lastik jelidir; lastik yüzeyine nüfuz eder, moleküler bağ kurar ve en az 4-5 yıkama boyunca saten siyahlığını korur. Sıçrama yapmayan jel formülü, yağmur-çamur dinlemez; lastiğin orijinal rengini yenilerken kir birikimini minimuma indirir.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

> SiO² Güçlü Formül — Seramik katkı uzun ömürlü hidrofobi ve UV koruması sağlar.
> Saten Doğal Bitiş — Yapay parlaklık yerine fabrika çıkışına yakın koyu görünüm.
> Derinlemesine Bağlanma — Jel, lastik gözeneklerine işler; 1 000 km+ kalıcılık.
> Sıçrama Yapmaz — Non-sling yapı; panel kirletmez.
> Katmanlanabilir — Isıtma veya ikinci kat ile dayanım uzatılabilir.
> Kolay Bakım — Kir, su ve tuz itici bariyer; temizleme süresini kısaltır.

Teknik Bilgiler

Parametre Değer Not
Tüketim / Seyreltme 10 – 15 ml / 1 araç Seyreltilmez
pH / SiO² pH etkisiz / SiO² bazlı Seramik hidrofobi

Ambalaj 500 ml jel şişe TireApplicator önerilir

Nasıl Kullanılır?

1. Temizlik – Lastiği Q²M TireCleaner + fırça ile derinlemesine temizleyin, tamamen kurutun.
2. Çalkala – Şişeyi iyice çalkalayın.
3. Uygula – TireApplicator’a 3-5 damla damlatın, ince ve eşit film hâlinde sürün.
4. Kuruma – 10-15 dk dokunmayın; fazla ürünü mikrofiberle hafifçe silin.
5. Isıt (Opsiyonel) – Isı tabancasıyla yanakları 40-50 °C’ye kadar ısıtıp ürünü emdirin.
6. İkinci Kat – Daha mat & uzun ömür için 20 dk sonra ikinci kat uygulayın.
7. Bekleme – Uygulamadan sonra aracı ? 2 saat kullanmayın.

• Show-car detayları ve günlük sürüş bakımı
• Motorsport / off-road lastik koruması

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ)

S: Parlak mı yoksa mat mı bırakır?
C: Tek kat saten-mat; ısıtma yapmadan ikinci kat hafif parlaklık katabilir.
S: Yağmurlu havada kalıcılığı düşer mi?
C: Hayır. SiO² bariyer su sıçramasına ve basınçlı yıkamaya karşı dirençlidir.
S: Kahverengileşme (blooming) yapar mı?
C: Yapmaz. UV filtreleri lastiğin renk stabilitesini korur.
S: Beyaz yazılı yanaklarda güvenli mi?
C: Evet; jel formül beyaz lastik harflerini sarartmaz.

Lastiklerinizi koruyun, renklerini canlandırın! Uygula, bekle ve yola çık — profesyonel lastik bakımı artık herkesin elinde!

### Teknik Özellikler
| Özellik | Değer |
|---------|-------|
| Durability Washes | 5+ Yıkama |
| Composition | SiO2 emdirilmiş |
| Finish Effect | Saten (Isıtılırsa parlak) |
| Features | Kir tutmaz, sıçrama yapmaz |
| Tüketim (ml/araç) | 12 |

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Lastiği Q²M TireCleaner + fırça ile derinlemesine temizleyin, tamamen kurutun.
2. Şişeyi iyice çalkalayın.
3. TireApplicator'a 3-5 damla damlatın, ince ve eşit film hâlinde sürün.
4. 10-15 dk dokunmayın; fazla ürünü mikrofiberle hafifçe silin.
5. Opsiyonel: Isı tabancasıyla yanakları 40-50°C'ye kadar ısıtıp ürünü emdirin.
6. İkinci kat için 20 dk sonra tekrar uygulayın.
7. Uygulamadan sonra aracı 2 saat kullanmayın.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Lastik yanaklarında uzun ömürlü saten siyahlık, UV koruması ve kir tutmama için kullanılır.

Consumption: 10-15ml / 1 set
Durability: >5 washes

How to Use

Step 1: Clean the Tires

Before applying Gyeon Q2 Tire, it's important to make sure that the tires are clean and dry. We recommend using a high-quality tire cleaner and a tire brush to remove any dirt, grime, or brake dust from the surface. Rinse the tires thoroughly and dry them with a clean microfiber towel.

Step 2: Apply Gyeon Tire Cleaner

Apply Gyeon Tire Cleaner to the tire and scrub it with a tire brush until it turns white. Rinse it thoroughly with water and dry it with a clean microfiber towel.

Step 3: Shake the Bottle

Shake the bottle of Gyeon Q2 Tire well before use to ensure that the formula is thoroughly mixed and ready to apply.

Step 4: Apply the Coating

Apply Gyeon Q2 Tire to the tire using a foam applicator pad. Use a small amount of the product and apply it in a thin, even layer. Make sure to cover the entire tire and avoid applying too much product to prevent streaks.

Advanced quartz technology combined with user friendly characteristics

DURABLE

ADVICE ON APPLICATION AND PRECAUTIONS

Before you start applying, wash the tire (a strong degreaser is recommended). Make sure that the surface is clean and dry. To increase durability, heat after application with a heatgun or hairdryer. Keep out of reach of children. Seek medical attention if swallowed.

FAQ

How long does it last?
When properly applied (we recommend two coats), it will last up to 10 washes, translating to 2-3 months of durability.

Is it shiny, satin or matte?
GYEON Tire will produce a satin finish but can be further buffed down to a light satin. It will dull down over time to a deep matte finish.

What's the difference between Tire and Tire Express?
Tire Express is water-based and can be applied while the tires are still wet. It's meant to be used as a 'fast dressing' and does not require preparation as thorough as GYEON Tire. Tire Express can also be used on other rubber surfaces, such as weather seals, to restore and protect them.

Will it sling?
No, it will not sling. The reason why something will sling is if too much product is applied without buffing it down. Also, ensure there are no products in the tire treads; make sure those are cleaned up as well.

Anything else I need to know?
A little goes a long way; just a few drops of GYEON Tire can coat an entire tire. You can also use this on other rubber pieces, such as weather seals, to rehydrate and protect from cracking.
TIP: The product can be applied thick on tires and left to soak in for a few hours before coming back to level it off.

### Detaylı Açıklama
GYEON Q² AntiFog Cam Buğu Önleyici Kaplama Seti - 120 ml

GYEON Q² AntiFog, araç içi camlarda buğulanmayı tek adımda ortadan kaldıran seramik destekli hidrofilik kaplamadır. 120 ml’lik şişesiyle 2 aya kadar kesintisiz berraklık sunar; soğuk, nemli havalarda dahi sürüş güvenliğinizi artırır.

Nasıl Uygulanır?

Hazırlık – Camı Q²M Glass ile temizle, ardından Q²M Prep ile yağdan arındır.
Ekipmanı Hazırla – Süet bezi aplikatöre sar, 5-6 damla Q² AntiFog damlat.

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ)

Soru: Renkli cam filmi üzerinde güvenli mi?
Cevap: Evet, tintli camlarda sprey-sil yöntemiyle uygulanabilir.
Soru: AntiFog cam temizleyici yerine geçer mi?
Cevap: Hafif kirde evet, ancak en iyi performans için önce cam temizleyici kullanın.
Soru: Tek kat ne kadar süre korur?
Cevap: Ortalama 2 ay; yoğun nemli iklimlerde gerekirse daha sık tazeleyin.
Soru: Plexi veya LCD ekrana uygulayabilir miyim?
Cevap: Evet, çiziksiz yüzeylerde güvenlidir.

İç camlardaki buğu derdine son verin, GYEON Q² AntiFog ile yolunuzu daima net görün!

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Camı Q²M Glass ile temizleyin, ardından Q²M Prep ile yağdan arındırın.
2. Süet bezi aplikatöre sarın, 5-6 damla Q² AntiFog damlatın.
3. Bölge bölge dairesel hareketlerle ince film oluşturun.
4. 5 dk kürleşme bekleyin; yüzeyde hafif pus oluşması normaldir.
5. Kısa tüylü veya nemli BaldWipe bezle kalıntıyı alın, iz bırakmayın.
6. Yoğun nemde buğu yeniden belirdiğinde tek kat tazeleme yeterlidir.

C: Evet, çiziksiz yüzeylerde güvenlidir.

## GYEON Q Booster 30 ml Seramik Yenileyici Hidrofobik Kaplama (SKU: Q2-BS30M)

### Detaylı Açıklama
GYEON Q² Booster Seramik Yenileyici Hidrofobik Kaplama - 30 ml

GYEON Q² Booster, mevcut seramik kaplamaları “profesyonel seviye” parlaklık ve ekstra hidrofobi ile güçlendiren tek katlık bir top-coat’tur. 120°’ye varan temas açısı, suyu ve kiri uzak tutar; kaplamanızın ömrünü 12 aya kadar uzatırken yüzeye ipeksi kayganlık katar.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

Evrensel Üst Kat – Q², SiO² veya rakip tüm seramiklerle tam uyumlu.
120°+ Hidrofobi – Aşırı boncuklanma, su lekesi riskini azaltır.
+12 Ay Dayanım – Kaplamanızın korumasını ve beading performansını yeniler.
Kendini Temizleyen Film – Anti-statik yapı, kir tutunmasını minimuma indirir.
Hızlı Uygulama – Tek kat, anında silme; çocuk oyuncağı kadar kolay.

Teknik Bilgiler

Parametre Değer Not
Tüketim 30 ml / araç 30 ml şişe = 1 araç
Dayanım +12 ay Taze kaplamada
pH 2 – 11 Asit-baz şampuanlara direnç
Temas Açısı ? 120 ° Ekstrem hidrofobi
Çalışma Sıcaklığı 10 – 30 °C Düşük nem, gölge ortam

Nasıl Uygulanır?

Hazırlık – Baz kaplama “kuru ama kürleşmemiş” (< 14 gün) olmalı; yüzeyi Q²M Prep ile yağdan arındır.
Ekipmanı Hazırla – Süet bez + blok; 6-8 damla Booster damlat.
Criss-Cross Uygulama – Paneli çapraz hareketlerle ince film hâlinde kapla.
Terleme & Silme – Ürün hızla buharlaşır; hemen BaldWipe ile hafifçe sil, iz bırakma.
Kürleşme – 2 saat toz-su temasından koru; tam kür 24 saat.
Bakım – Düzenli pH-nötr yıkama; 12 ay sonra gerekirse yeniden uygula.

Kullanım Alanları

– Taze uygulanmış Q² One / Pure / Mohs kaplamaları
– Kaplamanın beading gücünü yitirdiği filo & günlük araçlar
– Metal detaylar, krom çıtalar ve jantlarda su-kir iticiliği
– Anti-graffiti veya kolay temizlenen endüstriyel yüzeyler

Neden GYEON Q² Booster?

• Hidrofobi Şampiyonu – 120° temas açısı, göz alıcı beading sağlar.
• Çizgi Filmsiz Uygulama – Hızlı buharlaşma, hafif silme yeterli.
• Kimyasal Kalkan – pH 2-11 direnciyle sert şampuanlardan korkmaz.
• Esnek & Katmanlanabilir – Tüm markaların seramikleriyle çalışır, 1 saat sonra 2. kat atılabilir.

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ)

Soru: Booster tek başına koruma sağlar mı?
Cevap: Hayır; yalnızca mevcut seramik kaplamanın üzerine üst kat olarak kullanılır.
Soru: Baz kaplama kaç günlükken uygulanmalı?
Cevap: En iyi kimyasal bağ için kaplama 1 saat kurumuş, 14 günden genç olmalıdır.
Soru: İkinci kat gerekli mi?
Cevap: Çoğu durumda tek kat yeterlidir; daha fazla slick hissi için 1 saat sonra 2. kat atılabilir.
Seramik kaplamanızı tazeleyin; GYEON Q² Booster ile su iticiliği ve parlaklığı şimdi geri kazanın!

### Teknik Özellikler
| Özellik | Değer |
|---------|-------|
| Dayanım (Ay) | 12 |
| Function | Mevcut seramiğin hidrofobisini yenileme |
| Temas Açısı | >120° |
| Uygulama Yüzeyi | Kürleşmiş Seramik Üzeri |
| pH Toleransı | 2-11 |
| Tüketim (ml/araç) | 30 |

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Baz kaplama kuru ama kürleşmemiş (<14 gün) olmalı; yüzeyi Q²M Prep ile yağdan arındırın.
2. Süet bez + blok hazırlayın; 6-8 damla Booster damlatın.
3. Paneli çapraz hareketlerle ince film hâlinde kaplayın.
4. Ürün hızla buharlaşır; hemen BaldWipe ile hafifçe silin, iz bırakmayın.
5. 2 saat toz-su temasından koruyun; tam kür 24 saat.
6. Düzenli pH-nötr yıkama; 12 ay sonra gerekirse yeniden uygulayın.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Mevcut seramik kaplamaların hidrofobisini güçlendirmek, parlaklığı artırmak ve kaplamanın ömrünü uzatmak için kullanılır.

### Hedef Yüzeyler
Taze uygulanmış Q² One/Pure/Mohs kaplamaları, beading gücünü yitiren filo araçları, metal detaylar, krom çıtalar, jantlar

### Neden Bu Ürün?
• >120° temas açısı - ekstrem hidrofobi
• +12 ay dayanım ekler
• Tüm SiO² seramiklerle uyumlu
• Hızlı uygulama - tek kat yeterli

## GYEON Q Yüzey Koruyucu Antibakteriyel Seramik Kaplama (SKU: Q2-PC100M)

**Barkod:** 8809973750354
**Fiyat:** 1.800,00 TL
**Kategori:** İÇ YÜZEY > Detaylı Temizlik ve Bakım Ürünleri > Kumaş Koruyucular

### Kısa Açıklama
GYEON Q Yüzey Koruyucu Antibakteriyel Seramik Kaplama, 100 ml. Yüzeyleri korur, antibakteriyel etki sunar ve mükemmel otomobil bakımı sağlar.

### Detaylı Açıklama
GYEON Q² PurifyCoat – Antibakteriyel İç Yüzey Seramik Kaplama (100 ml)

TEK UYGULAMADA 12 AY BOYUNCA BAKTERİLERE KARŞI KALKAN OLUŞTURUN!

GYEON Q² PurifyCoat, her türlü iç yüzeyde bakteri ve mikrop oluşumunu önlemek için benzersiz bir seramik kaplama teknolojisinden yararlanır. Q² PurifyCoat, atomik düzeyde işlevselleştirilmiş SiO² + Cu²? formülüyle plastik, deri ve kumaşlara görünmez bir anti-mikrobiyal film bırakır. Alkolsüz, 0 doğal bileşenler sayesinde sağlıkla uyumlu; yüzeyde mat, fabrika çıkışı dokuyu korur.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

> 12 Ay Antibakteriyel Bariyer — Mikropların çoğalmasını engeller, kötü koku oluşumunu azaltır.
> SiO² + Mikro-Bakır Teknolojisi — Kalıcı etkili, solventsiz seramik ağ.
> Doğal Mat Bitiş — Parlaklık eklemez, renk değişimi yapmaz.
> Çok Yönlü Koruma — Plastik trim, deri koltuk, kumaş döşeme ve direksiyon dâhil.
> UV & Oksidasyon Direnci — Renk solmasını yavaşlatır, materyal ömrünü uzatır.
> Solvent & Alkol İçermez — Araç, ev, tekne ve ofis ortamlarında güvenle kullanılır.

Teknik Bilgiler

Parametre Değer Not
Tüketim / Seyreltme 10 ml / m² 100 ml şişe ? 2 orta sedan içi
SiO² İçeriği Fonksiyonel nano-silika Antibakteriyel matris
Aktif Metal Cu²? < 0.5 % Uzun ömürlü etki
Dayanıklılık ? 12 ay Doğru bakımda
Çalışma Sıcaklığı 15 – 30 °C Nemi düşük ortam
Kuruma / Kür 30 dk toz-temas 12 saat tam kür

Nasıl Kullanılır?

1. Hazırlık — Yüzeyi Q²M LeatherCleaner / InteriorDetailer ile temizleyip tamamen kurutun.
2. Uygulama — MF Applicator’a birkaç damla dökün; dairesel hareketlerle yaydıktan sonra paralel çizgilerle bitirin. Basınç uygulamayın.
3. Bekleme — 5-10 dk film oluşumuna izin verin.
4. Son Silme — Mikrofiber bezle nazikçe tek geçiş yapın. Yüksek nokta görürseniz yeniden uygulayıp hemen silin.
5. Kür — 12 saat pencere açık havalandırın; su/kimyasal temastan kaçının.
6. Bakım — Her 2-3 ayda bir Q²M PurifyMaintain ile tazeleme spreyi.

Kullanım Alanları

• Araç içi plastik, vinil, piyano black trim
• Nappa / sentetik deri koltuk ve direksiyon
• Kumaş koltuk, paspas ve bagaj halısı
• Ev-ofis mobilya kumaşı, çocuk koltuğu, evcil hayvan yatağı
• Denizcilik kabin yüzeyleri ve RV iç mekânlar

Neden GYEON Q² PurifyCoat?

• Hijyen Standardı — COVID sonrası dönemde kabin sağlığına kalıcı çözüm.
• Uzun Vadeli Tasarruf — Sık dezenfektan kullanım ihtiyacını azaltır.
• Güvenli & Ekolojik — Uçucu organik bileşik içermez, alerjen oluşturmaz.
• Profesyonel veya DIY — Kolay aplikatör, hızlı kür; atölye portföyünü genişletir.

A: Hayır, mat bitiş şeffaftır; parlak yüzeyde yansıma derecesini değiştirmez.

A: 0 doğal, alkol & VOC içermeyen formül çocuk ekipmanlarında güvenle kullanılabilir.

A: En az 7 gün bekleyin; krem katmanı PurifyCoat’ın nefes almasını engelleyebilir.
Q: Buharlı temizleyici kaplamaya zarar verir mi?
A: 100 °C üzeri sıcaklık maruziyeti direnci düşürebilir; ılık nemli bez tercih edin.

## GYEON Q One EVO 30 ml Seramik Kaplama (SKU: Q2-OLE30M)

**Barkod:** 8809432672449
**Fiyat:** 1.950,00 TL
**Kategori:** DIŞ YÜZEY > Seramik Kaplama Ürünleri > Seramik Kaplamalar

### Kısa Açıklama
GYEON Q One EVO 30 ml Seramik Kaplama - MTS Kimya güvencesiyle orijinal ve güvenli alışveriş fırsatıyla satın alın. 9H koruma ve su itici etki sağlayın.

### Detaylı Açıklama
GYEON Q² One EVO Light Box Araç Seramik Kaplama - 30 ml - 9H Oto Boya Koruma-Su İtici

GYEON Q² One EVO Light Box, tek kat uygulamada 24 ay veya 25.000 km’ye varan dayanım sunan, yüksek parlaklık ve müthiş boncuklama özelliğine sahip SiO² bazlı EVO versiyonudur. Zararlı UV ışınlarından korur, kimyasallara (pH 2–11) dirençlidir ve dış etkenlere karşı kolay temizlenebilirlik kazandırır.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

> 24 Ay / 25.000 km Dayanım — Geliştirilmiş EVO formülü, uzun soluklu koruma sağlar.
> Mükemmel Boncuklama — Yağmur ve yıkama sularını hızla iterek self-cleaning etkisi yaratır.
> Yüksek Parlaklık — Candy gloss görünümüyle boyanın derin rengini ön plana çıkarır.
> Geniş pH Toleransı — pH 2–11 arası kimyasallara karşı üstün direnç.
> Tek Kat Uygulama — Pratik Light Box kiti, her metrekare yüzeyi kaplayacak dozajda.
> UV & Kimyasal Kalkan — Zararlı güneş ışınlarına ve yıkama deterjanlarına karşı bariyer oluşturur.

Teknik Bilgiler

Parametre	Değer	Not
Kapasite	30 ml	25–30 ml / araç
Dayanım	24 ay / 25.000 km	Düzenli bakım ile uzar
pH Tolerans	2 – 11	Kimyasal direnç, asit ve baz testleri geçerli
Tüketim	25–30 ml / araç	Coating Applicator Mini ile homojen uygulama
Çalışma Sıcaklığı	5 – 30 °C	Direkt güneşten ve yüksek nemden kaçının
Ambalaj	Light Box seti (Mini aplikatör, etiket, kılavuz)	Uygulama kolaylığı için ideal kit formatı

Nasıl Kullanılır?

1.	Yüzey Hazırlığı
• Aracı yıkayın; gerekirse kil ve polisaj ile kontaminantları giderin.
• Q²M Prep ile boya ve cila kalıntılarını tamamen silin.
• Yüzeyin toz, su lekesi ve parlatıcı artıklarından arındığından emin olun.
2.	Hazırlık & Damlatma
• Coating Applicator Mini bloğunu Q²M Suede ile sarın.
• Pipete 6–8 damla Q² One EVO damlatın (her panel için).
• Kapağın sıkı kapalı, pipetin temiz ve kuru olduğuna dikkat edin.
3.	Çapraz Serpme (Panel Bazlı)
• Omuz genişliği (?50×50 cm) alan seçin.
• Önce dikey, sonra yatay geçişlerle ince, homojen bir film oluşturun.
• Yüzey hâlâ ıslak ve eşit dağılmışsa uygulama tamamdır.
4.	Terleme Takibi
• 30–120 sn içinde yüzey “terleyip” ince küçük boncuklar oluşturur.
• Işık altında hafif sis (hafifıslak parlaklık) görünce silme vaktidir.
5.	Silme & Parlatma
• 1. Bez: Q²M BaldWipe ile nazikçe, dairesel hareketlerle kalıntıları alın.
• 2. Bez: Q²M SoftWipe ile tek yönlü silerek candy gloss’u ortaya çıkarın.
• Spot ışık ile paneli kontrol edin; iz veya leke varsa anında düzeltin.
6.	Kürleşme
• Aracı en az 12 saat kuru, tozsuz ve gölgeli bir ortamda bekletin.
• İlk 7 gün deterjan kullanmayın; isteğe bağlı IR lamba (60 °C × 10 dk) süreci hızlandırır.
7.	İkinci Kat (Opsiyonel)
• İlk katın üzerinden ? 60 dk sonra aynı adımlarla ince kat uygulayın.
• İkinci kat, ekstra hidrofobi ve parlaklık sağlar.
8.	İlk Bakım & Koruma
• Uygulamadan 1 saat sonra Q²M Cure ile üst katmanı güçlendirin.
• Rutin yıkamalarda Q²M CeramicDetailer veya Q²M WetCoat ile performansı tazeleyin.

Kullanım Alanları

• Otomotiv tüm boyalı yüzeyler (kaporta, tavan, motor kaputu)
• Motosiklet ve bisiklet çerçeveleri
• Cam ve parlak plastik aksesuarlar
• Tekne güvertesi ve kaplama panelleri
• Ev dış cephe panelleri ve ofis giriş kaplamaları

Neden GYEON Q² One EVO Light Box?

• Kolay & Hızlı – Tek kat, küçük alanlarda bile tutarlı uygulama garantisi.
• Üstün Performans – EVO vsiyonu 0 daha fazla kimyasal dirence sahip.
• Ekonomik – 30 ml ile bir araç yüzeyi sertifikalı şekilde kaplanır.
• Self-Cleaning Etki – Temizleme aralıklarını uzatır, bakım maliyetini düşürür.

Önerilen Aksesuar & Tamamlayıcı Ürünler

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ)

S: Light Box ile 50 ml versiyon arasındaki fark nedir?
C: İçerik aynıdır; sadece paket içeriği ve applicator boyutu farklıdır.

C: Evet, ikinci kat için min. 1 saat bekleyip ince tabaka sürün.

C: 12 saat sonra su ve toz temasına açıktır; tam sertleşme 14 gün sürer.

# Gyeon Q² One EVO Light\n\nBrand: Gyeon\nPrice: \u00a335.00\n30 ml - \u00a335.00\n50 ml - \u00a349.00\nAvailability: Only 10 left!\n\n\n\n\n## We Say\n\nThe Light versions of Gyeons coatings are no different to their regular coatings, the only difference is they contain the coatings only. These are great for those that don't require the extra bits included. In the case of Q2 One Light, it doesn't contain the Q2M Cure. If you require the full kit, it can be found here: Gyeon Q2 One EVO.\n\n## Key Features\n\nBeading: 8/10 (Compared To Others)\nDurability: 24 Months (Average Value)\nSlickness: 8/10 (Compared To Others)\n\n## Description\n\nGyeon Q² One EVO Light is a user-friendly quartz coating that simultaneously protects and enhances the appearance of automotive paint. Developed in South Korea, Gyeon Q² One EVO Light uses the latest in low volatile content silicon (Si) technology to lay down a film of pure siloxane polymers that condense rapidly to form a fully crystallized SiO2 coating that bonds to painted surfaces at the molecular level. Unlike many coatings, Gyeon Q² One EVO Light contains no alcohol and therefore doesn't flash off rapidly, which makes the application process much easier. Furthermore, because it is designed to be wiped on and then wiped off immediately, it is no harder to apply than a natural carnauba wax. Nevertheless, despite how easy it is to use, Gyeon Q² One EVO Light features significantly more SiO2 than is usually the case for entry level coatings, which gives it class leading durability at a very affordable price point.\n\nAs a result of being coated with a smooth, dense layer of crystallized SiO2, treated surfaces become extremely hydrophobic (water-hating), which causes rainfall and rinse water to bead up and roll off very quickly. This extreme beading not only looks good, but also tends to pick up and carry away fresh contaminants, which makes routine washing easier and much safer. In addition to these benefits, Gyeon Q² One EVO Light also provides high levels of protection against bird droppings, bug splatter, road salt and harmful UV radiation for up to twelve months, even on daily drivers (it is virtually impervious to cleaning chemicals and pressure washing). Gyeon Q² One EVO Light is currently supplied as a pre-packed kit containing either a 30 ml or 50 ml bottle of Gyeon Q² One EVO, a Gyeon Q²M Applicator, Stickers and an instruction booklet.\n\n## Specification\n\n| Adds Protection | Yes |\n| Application Method | By hand only |\n| Beading | 8 |\n| Durability | 24 months |\n| Emits Strong Fumes | Yes |\n| Enhances Gloss | Yes |\n| Flake Pop | 10 |\n| Glossiness | 9 |\n| Hardness | 7 |\n| Layerable | Yes (allow 1 hour between coats) |\n| Recommended For | All paint types and colours |\n| Reflectivity | 10 |\n| Richness | 7 |\n| Scratch Resistant | Yes |\n| Slickness | 8 |\n| Trim-Safe | No |\n\n## How To Use\n\nYou should apply Gyeon Q² One EVO Light in a dry place out of direct sunlight. In all cases, prepare the surfaces you are going to treat in the normal way (wash > decontaminate > polish), and then do a wipe down with Gyeon Q²M Prep to ensure that they are spotlessly clean. Next, wrap a Gyeon Q²M Applicator Suedes around a Gyeon Q²M Applicator Block and lightly wet one end of it with Gyeon Q² One using the supplied dropping pipette. Then spread the coating quickly over the first panel, using light pressure and overlapping strokes. After 20-30 seconds, and without adding any more product, rub the Gyeon Q²M Applicator Suede over the panel in tight circles, using moderate speed and pressure. This step is critical, as it levels the coating and makes it easy to remove. You must then buff off the remaining residue as quickly as possible, i.e. before it begins to harden. Buffing off is best accomplished with a PB Super Buffing Towel using moderate speed and pressure in order to fully remove the residue and reveal an intense streak-free shine. Using a bright light, check the panel carefully for smears and remove them before moving on; failure to remove smears fully can result in them hardening to the point of being impossible to remove without machine polishing, so make sure you are thorough!\n\nAfter all panels are treated you must then leave the car in a dry place out of direct sunlight for a minimum of 24 hours to allow the SiO2 coating to harden (if you wish, you can accelerate this process by heating the treated panels to 60\u00b0C for 10 minutes using an infra-red heat lamp). Finally, to reduce the risk of water spots forming while it continues to cure (full curing takes around 14 days to achieve), you should apply a protective topcoat of Gyeon Q²M Cure (you should also avoid washing the car with any kind of detergent for the first 7 days). Please note that you must discard all used applicators and towels after you've applied Gyeon Q² One, because it hardens massively as it cures, forming a residue that has the potential to inflict severe marring or worse if applicators and towels are re-used. Furthermore, after each use you must also replace the dropping pipette with the air-tight cap, and then wash out the pipette with hot water. Failure to follow these steps will result in any leftover product setting solid in the bottle and the pipette, rendering them unusable in the future.

Wipe off immediately with either the Q²M SoftWipe or Q²M PolishWipe. Q² One EVO builds a thick layer, so you will need an absorbent towel.\nTIP: The choice of towels for coating wipe off is extremely important. Do not stick to just one type - depending on paint and climate, even the Q²M Suede might be the best choice for perfecting the surface.\n\n## Decon\nDecontaminating the paint is key to proper coating adhesion.\n\n## Prep\nThe Prep removes any polish oils and any other residues left over or missed.\n\n## Maintenance\nMaintenance is key to keeping your coating performing at its maximum.\n\n\n\n## WHY GYEON ONE EVO?\nOne EVO combines the advantages of all forms of protection. A high water contact angle of over 110' results in spectacular water behaviour and helps with regular maintenance.\n\n### SUPERB SELF-CLEANING ABILITIES\nOne of the key characteristics of Q² One, especially when compared with other protective coatings, is its excellent self-cleaning ability. This ability can significantly extend the intervals between washes. Of course, the coating does not remain perfectly clean after a long drive in bad weather, but it does considerably help, and also makes it a lot easier to safely remove residual dirt afterwards.\n\n### ADVICE ON APPLICATION AND PRECAUTIONS\nBefore you start applying make sure that the surface is oil free and completely dry. It is recommended to wash the car with Q²M Bathe, use Q²M Iron and Q²M Tar to remove impurities and degrease with Q²M Prep. Skin protection recommended. Work in a well-ventilated area. Store in a dark, dry and cool place. Keep out of reach of children. Never apply in direct sunlight.\n\nAll GYEON products does not contain any Per- and Polyfluoroalkyl Substances (PFAS / 'forever chemicals') as defined or restricted under the relevant Canadian environmental and chemical management regulations, including but not limited to:\n- The Canadian Environmental Protection Act, 1999 (CEPA) and its associated\n- Prohibition of Certain Toxic Substances Regulations, 2012 (SOR/2012-285), as amended;\n- The Domestic Substances List and Non-domestic Substances List under CEPA;\n- Any applicable federal or provincial restrictions pertaining to PFAS substances.\n\n### Outdoor-friendly application\nAll EVO formulas can be applied outdoors. Ensure stable conditions, never use in direct sunlight and check the weather forecast! The coating should not get wet in the first 12 hours after application.\n\n### Easy & Durable\nWith the introduction of EVO formulas, applying Q² One EVO is now even simpler than before. It offers significantly enhanced durability, improved by 50% compared to its previous version. The increased performance and higher chemical resistance make it an excellent entry-level coating for enthusiasts.\n\n### Glossy & Hydrophobic\nWith its superb beading, Q² One EVO meets all the expectations of car care enthusiasts. However, beading would mean nothing without the intense candy gloss.\n\n### One EVO vs GYEON's other coating\nGYEON One EVO is perfect for first-timers, offering a balance of cost and effectiveness without compromising quality. If you're new to coating or transitioning from wax/sealant applications, One EVO is an ideal choice. It's easy to apply with minimal risk of leaving 'high spots.'\n\n## GYEON ONE EVO FAQs\n\nHow long does it last?\nThis depends on several factors. Is the vehicle primarily used in the summer or winter? How frequently is it maintained and topped up with Gyeon Cure or Gyeon Ceramic Detailer? For our Canadian climate, we often recommend applying two layers. While this won't double the coating's longevity, it can still provide a significant boost, around 20% or more, compared to a single-layer application.\nSince the vehicle is already clean and prepped, it's a good idea to apply a second layer. While the preparation process may take some time, the application itself is straightforward. Below is the timeframe under monthly maintenance with Gyeon Cure or Gyeon Ceramic Detailer:\n- Summer driven only (garage kept): at least 24 months or beyond\n- Summer driven with no garage: ~24 months\n- Winter driven only (garage kept): 18 to 24 months\n- Winter/Daily driven with no garage: ~12 months\n- Daily driven (garage kept): ~18 months\nIn winter, maintenance becomes crucial for its longevity for daily/winter-driven cars. Without regular maintenance or reapplication during the winter months (understandably challenging in -30\u00b0C weather), you may notice wear and deterioration on the lower sections due to road salts, chemicals, contaminants, and other factors. After a thorough decontamination, water beading may return, but it's not uncommon for the lower sections to show signs of wear after winter. This is particularly true given the harshness of our winters, at least here in Canada. The key takeaway is that the coating is designed to wear off first, protecting the paint beneath.\n\nWhen do I wipe it off?\nThis depends on the ambient temperature, but it is recommended to wipe off within the first 10 to 30 seconds after applying to the entire panel/section. If the room temperature is higher, work section by section. If cooler, proceed panel by panel. You have up to a 5-minute wipe-off window to return and check your work, ensuring you haven't missed any spots.\n\nWhat's the layering time?\nWe typically recommend waiting between 2 to 4 hours between layers, but it's best not to exceed 24 hours. The reason for this is that if you wait too long, you'll be applying the second layer onto a surface that has already hardened and become slick, and the bonding won't be as effective. On the other hand, if you apply the second layer too quickly, the solvents in the second layer can soften the first layer, essentially merging them into one. Ideally, you want to apply the second layer when the first layer is still in the process of curing, so they can bond cohesively. You want the coating to be both physically layerable and able to bond well at the same time.\n\nHow much will the bottle do?\nWith the new EVOs, a 30ml bottle can equate to a 50ml bottle of the previous-gen product. For a mid-sized vehicle, such as a Camry, you can expect to use approximately 15ml per layer. A mid-sized SUV will require around 20ml, and a full-sized truck will typically use between 25 to 30ml. It's important to note that applying two coats does make a noticeable difference.\n\nWhat can I layer it with?\nYou can layer One EVO with another layer of One EVO or CanCoat EVO. The general rule of thumb is to apply the most durable product first and the slicker product on top. A popular combination, for the best of both worlds, using One EVO as the first layer (providing the candy gloss finish) and then applying CanCoat EVO on top because it's a slicker product that can efficiently repel dirt.\n\nAfter coating, when can I take the vehicle out?\nA general rule of thumb is to avoid water contact for 24 to 48 hours and refrain from using soap for a week. However, after the coating is applied, you can take the vehicle out immediately. Dust, dew, and wind won't have much effect, but it's important to be mindful of bugs, which can impact the finish. If you're a business coating a vehicle for a customer, and it must be exposed to water within the next 12 hours, you can very gently wipe it down with Gyeon Cure or Gyeon Ceramic Detailer. We still recommend against it, but sometimes it's necessary. It's important to understand that drying and curing are distinct processes. While the coating or panel may feel dry to the touch right away, curing involves the molecular locking process, and it requires time to fully cure.\n\nHow cold (or hot) can I apply the coating under?\nA temperature of at least 10\u00b0C is recommended, although you can still attempt the application between 5\u00b0C to 10\u00b0C if necessary. If the temperature reaches 30\u00b0C, then it's on the warmer side, and you will need to retreat into the shade. Ideally, you want the coating to remain on the panel for at least 30 to 60 seconds without flashing right away. If it flashes within that time, it's likely that the panel is too hot.\n\nCan I apply the coating outdoors?\nAbsolutely, all the new Gyeon EVO coatings can be applied outdoors; just be mindful of the temperature, as mentioned in the question above.\n\nWhat do I maintain it with and how often?\nYou can use products like Gyeon WetCoat, Cure, Ceramic Detailer, etc., as frequently as you'd like. The only thing to caution about is using waxes on your coating (Gyeon Wax is fine) because most waxes have strong solvents that may affect the coating.\n\nI have a 'high-spot', what do I do?\nHigh spots refer to dried coatings that were not completely buffed off. If you catch the high spots within 30 minutes, you can use the coating itself again to level/soften the high spots. If it's been a few days, then you'll need to mechanically polish it off or use Gyeon Total Remover to remove and reapply coating on the affected area.\n\nWhat can I wash it with afterwards?\nAny pH-neutral soap is suitable for use, and Gyeon recommends Bathe and Bathe+. Ideally, avoid using wash and 'wax' products. While you can use them, it's worth noting that a wash and 'wax' product tends to diminish the water-beading properties of your coating. This results in reduced hydrophobicity after washing. After all, who would want that?!\n\nWhat's the expiration date? New and opened.\nOfficially, Gyeon recommends the product to be used within 2 to 3 years when new. If the bottle has been opened, it's best to use up the product in 1 to 2 months to preserve the coating's maximum effectiveness.\n\nCan I apply it on PPF, Trim, Plastics, Wheels, Chrome and Windows?\nThe short answer is Yes.\nPPF: Since the material is more porous and grabbier, you'll need to wipe off the coating at a faster rate. It's best to use Gyeon PPF Coating.\nTrim & Plastics: Yes, though it will not darken and 'restore' like Gyeon Trim does.\nWheels, Chrome & Metal: Yes. You can also consider Gyeon's more cost-effective alternative for wheels, Gyeon Rim (also heat resistant).\nWindows: Technically yes, but avoid the front windshield, as certain wiper/washer fluid combos may chatter. Use Gyeon View or QuickView for chatter-free experience.\n\nCan it be shipped in the cold?\nNo problem at all. Coatings contain a significant amount of solvents and exhibit high chemical stability.

Nasıl Uygulanır?

1. Yüzey Hazırlığı
• Aracı yıkayın, gerekiyorsa kil + polisaj yapın.
• Tüm yağ/polisaj kalıntılarını Q²M Prep ile silin.
2. Hazırlık & Damlatma
• Aplikatör bloğunu süetle sarın; 6-8 damla ürün damlatın.
• Başlamadan önce kapak sıkıca kapalı, pipet temiz olmalı.
3. Çapraz Serpme (Panel Bazlı)
• Omuz genişliğinde alana önce dikey, sonra yatay pass’larla eşit yayılım.
• Yüzey hafif ıslak ve homogense uygulama tamamdır.
4. Terleme Takibi
• 30-120 sn içinde yüzey “terleyip” ince boncuklar oluşturur.
• Işık altında hafif sis göründüğünde silme vaktidir.
5. Silme & Parlatma
• 1. bez: Q²M BaldWipe ile kalıntıyı nazikçe alın.
• 2. bez: Q²M SoftWipe ile parlaklığı ortaya çıkarın.
• Paneli spot ışıkla kontrol edin; iz kalırsa anında düzeltin.
6. Kürleşme
• Araç en az 12 saat toz/sudan uzak, kuru ortamda kalsın.
• 7 gün deterjan kullanılmaz; IR lamba (60 °C × 10 dk) ile süreç hızlanabilir.
7. İkinci Kat (Opsiyonel)
• İlk katın üzerinden ? 60 dk sonra aynı adımları tekrarlayın.
8. İlk Bakım
• 1 saat sonra Q²M Cure ile üst katman; su lekesi riskini azaltır.
• Rutin yıkamalarda Q²M CeramicDetailer / WetCoat ile performansı tazeleyin.

• Premium Boya Koruması — Show-car parlaklığı + 5 yıl kalkan.
• Günlük Sürücüler — Kire, tuza, UV’ye karşı uzun soluklu bariyer.

**S: Tek kat yeterli mi?**

2.	Hazırlık & Damlatma
• Aplikatör bloğunu süetle sarın; 6-8 damla ürün damlatın.
• Başlamadan önce kapak sıkıca kapalı, pipet temiz olmalı.

• Omuz genişliğinde alana önce dikey, sonra yatay pass’larla eşit yayılım.

• 1. bez: Q²M BaldWipe ile kalıntıyı nazikçe alın.
• 2. bez: Q²M SoftWipe ile parlaklığı ortaya çıkarın.
• Paneli spot ışıkla kontrol edin; iz kalırsa anında düzeltin.
6.	Kürleşme
• Araç en az 12 saat toz/sudan uzak, kuru ortamda kalsın.
• 7 gün deterjan kullanılmaz; IR lamba (60 °C × 10 dk) ile süreç hızlanabilir.
7.	İkinci Kat (Opsiyonel)
• İlk katın üzerinden ? 60 dk sonra aynı adımları tekrarlayın.
8.	İlk Bakım
• 1 saat sonra Q²M Cure ile üst katman; su lekesi riskini azaltır.
• Rutin yıkamalarda Q²M CeramicDetailer / WetCoat ile performansı tazeleyin.

Q: Mat boyada parlaklık yapar mı?
A: Hayır. Mat dokuyu korur, görünümü değiştirmez.

### Web Kaynak İçerikleri
> Kaynak 1: https://gyeon.co/product/syncro-evo/

Q2 SYNCRO EVO

Exterior / coating

An advanced two-stage ceramic paint coating.

Q2 Syncro EVO is a two-stage coating system designed to provide maximum durability, gloss, and long-term protection. It combines Q2 Mohs EVO as a base layer with Q2 Skin EVO as a dedicated top coat. Together, they form a dense, smooth protective shell with excellent water repellency and enhanced color depth.

Second skin for your paint

Q2 Syncro EVO is designed for users seeking more than what a single-layer coating can provide. The system enhances durability, boosts self-cleaning capabilities, and adds visual depth, especially on darker colors. Its two-step process ensures consistent performance over time while maintaining controlled and predictable application.

SELF-CLEANING PROPERTIES
PREVENTS UV DAMAGE
GUARDS AGAINST THE ELEMENTS
WATER REPELLENT
OUTDOOR FRIENDLY APPLICATION

TECHNICAL DETAILS

CAPACITIES: 30 & 30 ML / 50 & 50 ML

BOX CONTAINS: Q2 MOHS EVO / Q2 SKIN EVO / Q2M COATING APPLICATOR / Q2M CURE 100ML / MANUAL / MAINTENANCE BOOKLET MINI / DOOR STICKERS / #GYEONIZED STICKER

LIGHTBOX CONTAINS: Q2 MOHS EVO / Q2 SKIN EVO / Q2M COATING APPLICATOR LIGHT / MANUAL / MAINTENANCE BOOKLET MINI / DOOR STICKERS / #GYEONIZED STICKER

Real World Lifespan: up to 50 MONTHS / 50KKM
PH Tolerance: 2-11
Consumption: 15-25ml/car

Instruction PDF:

HOW TO USE Q2 SYNCRO EVO

01. After polishing, wash the car using Q2M Degrease Tabs and hot water. Make sure the surface is clean.
02. Ensure the surface is oil-free and completely dry. Apply Q2M Prep. Wait 15 minutes.
03. Apply Q2 Mohs EVO as the base layer with the Q2M Coating Applicator. Ensure the surface is cool and free of dust.
04. After the base layer has been applied to the whole vehicle, evenly apply Q2 Skin EVO immediately as the top layer to improve gloss and water resistance.
05. For Q2 Mohs, wipe it off immediately. When the coating begins to "sweat," it's the ideal moment to wipe. For Q2 Skin, wipe off right away, within 10 to 30 seconds of applying.

FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS

01. Why does Q2 Syncro EVO use two layers?
The base layer gives strength and durability, while the top layer improves gloss and hydrophobic behaviour.

02. Is Q2 Syncro EVO harder to apply than a single coating?
It requires more time, but the process remains controlled and clear when following the steps.

03. Can it be applied outdoors?
Yes. Avoid direct sunlight and keep the surface dry during early curing.

04. Which paint colours benefit most from this system?
Dark colours show the biggest increase in depth and clarity.

05. How should I maintain the coating?
Use pH neutral shampoo and boost performance with Q2M Cure when needed.

Product Images:

Studio grade coating
Q2 Syncro EVO offers a unique opportunity to apply a specially designed coating system consisting of a sophisticated base coat, Q2 Mohs EVO, and the Q2 Skin EVO topcoat. This system significantly increases gloss and the durability of the hydrophobic effect. The topcoat also provides very strong color enhancement, particularly noticeable on dark-colored paints.

CONSUMPTION: 15-25ml/car
PH TOLERANCE: 2-11
DURABILITY: Up to 60 MONTHS / 50K KM+

BEST PRACTICE & PRO-TIPS
Apply Mohs EVO liberally first in your favourite motion to a whole panel. Once temperature and humidity rise, apply to smaller sections and wipe off immediately. The product will lightly bubble up on the panel - this is the perfect timing for wipe off.
Then apply Skin EVO 1~2 hours after Mohs EVO. Work on a 2 x 2' section at a time with Skin EVO and wipe off immediately.
TIP: For optimal results, apply two layers of Mohs EVO and one layer of Skin EVO. These are professional shop-grade coatings that are easy to apply by mere mortals!

Mohs EVO vs Syncro EVO
While Mohs EVO can be applied as a standalone product and layered on its own, but for optimal results, consider upgrading to Syncro Evo. Why, you ask? Skin EVO is specifically engineered to adhere seamlessly to a surface that's already slick. This synergy ensures enhanced bonding and superior chemical cohesion for both products.

Ceramic Coating kit GYEON Mohs + GYEON Skin

The most advanced ceramic coating for enthusiasts and detailing professionals. The sophisticated double-stage formula delivers great results with minimum effort. Q2 Syncro offers incredible slickness and repellency. The Q2 Mohs base provides hardness and significant durability. Q2 Skin is a thick and flexible topcoat that provides great self-cleaning abilities.

BOX CONTAINS: Q2 MOHS evo / Q2 SKIN evo / MANUAL

HARD AND SLICK
Q2 Mohs is the hardest automotive paint coating available to a wide range of users. The extraordinary hardness of the coating preserves the effects achieved with paint correction. Combined with the extreme slickness of the Q2 Skin topcoat, the Q2 Syncro coating system provides immense benefits during daily maintenance routines, making regular care less frequent and easier.

ADVANCED AND USER-FRIENDLY
Q2 Syncro is the most advanced widely available coating offered by Gyeon. Its aim is to give a professional coating experience to all customers outside the Certified Detailer Program. Its multilayer application ends with the application of the Q2 Skin, an advanced silicone-based topcoat that provides exceptional slickness and unrivalled hydrophobicity. Despite the three-layer application, both base and topcoat are user-friendly.

ADVICE ON APPLICATION AND PRECAUTIONS
Before you start applying make sure that the surface is oil free and completely dry. It is recommended to wash the car with Q2M Bathe, use Q2M Iron and Q2M Tar to remove impurities and degrease with Q2M Prep. Skin protection recommended. Work in a well-ventilated area. Store in a dark, dry and cool place. Keep out of reach of children. Avoid applying in direct sunlight.

CONSUMPTION: 30ml Skin + 50ml Mohs / Large vehicle. Generally 15ml Mohs per coat, times two. 20-25ml Skin, as it goes on thicker.

CONTACT ANGLE: >120'
PH TOLERANCE: 2-11
THICKNESS: 0,2 - 0,5qm

It's the Formulation
Q2 Mohs EVO uses fluoro modified polysilazanes for the first time in the car care industry. Why is that so important? Modifying polysilazanes at the precursory stages bring enormous benefits on all levels: durability, chemical resistance or ease of use. Amazingly easy to apply and wipe off, yet extremely chemical resistant. Slick and smooth, yet very durable. Gloss and extreme hydrophobic are just value-added.

Outdoor-friendly application
All EVO formulas can be applied outdoors. Ensure stable conditions, never use in direct sunlight and check the weather forecast! The coating should not get wet in the first 12 hours after application.

30ml = 50ml, 50ml = 80ml
The classic Q2 Mohs was known as a multilayer product. Its EVO version changes that and now allows a simple and very straightforward application with just one layer. Thanks to the formula, but also our Q2M CoatingApplicator, 30ml of the EVO formula equal at least 50ml of the retired, classic product delivering even improved performance.

GYEON Syncro EVO FAQs

How long does it last?
This depends on several factors. Is the vehicle primarily used in the summer or winter? How frequently is it maintained and topped up with Gyeon Cure or Gyeon Ceramic Detailer? For our Canadian climate, we often recommend applying two layers. While this won't double the coating's longevity, it can still provide a significant boost, around 20% or more, compared to a single-layer application. Since the vehicle is already clean and prepped, it's a good idea to apply a second layer. While the preparation process may take some time, the application itself is straightforward.
If the vehicle is only driven in the summer and receives monthly maintenance, then Syncro EVO can easily last for at least 5 years and beyond. However, if it's a daily driver used throughout the year, especially in the winter, maintenance becomes crucial for its longevity. Without regular maintenance or reapplication during the winter months (understandably challenging in -30C weather), you may notice wear and deterioration on the lower sections due to road salts, chemicals, contaminants, and other factors. After a thorough decontamination, water beading may return, but it's not uncommon for the lower sections to show signs of wear after winter. This is particularly true given the harshness of our winters, at least here in Canada. The key takeaway is that the coating is designed to wear off first, protecting the paint beneath.

When do I wipe it off?
This depends on ambient temperature. A good general rule of thumb is when you see Mohs EVO bubble up into little beads, then it's time to wipe it off, usually around 30 seconds. You don't need to rush the process and panic; just casually apply and wipe off in under a minute. Mohs EVO is a very easy product to work with. Tip: It should be fairly easy to buff off; if you feel it's getting a little too tacky, then you've waited too long.
Skin EVO is wipe on, wipe off, wait time between 5~30 seconds.

What's the layering time?
Indeed, layering is very much encouraged, but it's essential to find the right timing. We typically recommend waiting between 2 to 4 hours between layers, but it's best not to exceed 24 hours. The reason for this is that if you wait too long, you'll be applying the second layer onto a surface that has already hardened and become slick, and the bonding won't be as effective. On the other hand, if you apply the second layer too quickly, the solvents in the second layer can soften the first layer, essentially merging them into one. Ideally, you want to apply the second layer when the first layer is still in the process of curing, so they can bond cohesively. You want the coating to be both physically layerable and able to bond well at the same time.

How much will the bottle do?
With the new EVOs, a 30ml bottle can equate to a 50ml bottle of the previous-gen product. For a mid-sized vehicle, such as a Camry, you can expect to use approximately 15ml per layer. A mid-sized SUV will require around 20ml, and a full-sized truck will typically use between 25 to 30ml. It's important to note that applying two coats does make a noticeable difference.

What can I layer it with?
You can layer Mohs EVO with another layer of Mohs EVO, Skin EVO (from the Syncro EVO kit), or CanCoat EVO. The general rule of thumb is that you want the most durable product down first and the slicker product on top. A fairly popular combo, if you want the best of both worlds, is Pure EVO as the first layer (Pure EVO will provide the candy apple finish), then Mohs EVO on top because it's a slicker product that can shed off dirt more efficiently.

After coating, when can I take the vehicle out?
A general rule of thumb is to avoid water contact for 24 to 48 hours and refrain from using soap for a week. However, after the coating is applied, you can take the vehicle out immediately. Dust, dew, and wind won't have much effect, but it's important to be mindful of bugs, which can impact the finish. If you're a business coating a vehicle for a customer, and it must be exposed to water within the next 12 hours, you can very gently wipe it down with Gyeon Cure or Gyeon Ceramic Detailer. We still recommend against it, but sometimes it's necessary. It's important to understand that drying and curing are distinct processes. While the coating or panel may feel dry to the touch right away, curing involves the molecular locking process, and it requires time to fully cure.

How cold (or hot) can I apply the coating under?
A temperature of at least 10 degrees C is recommended, although you can still attempt the application between 5 degrees C to 10 degrees C if necessary. If the temperature reaches 30 degrees C, then it's on the warmer side, and you will need to retreat into the shade. Ideally, you want the coating to remain on the panel for at least 30 to 60 seconds without flashing right away. If it flashes within that time, it's likely that the panel is too hot.

Can I apply the coating outdoors?
Absolutely, all the new Gyeon EVO coatings can be applied outdoors; just be mindful of the temperature, as mentioned in the question above.

What do I maintain it with and how often?
You can use products like Gyeon WetCoat, Cure, Ceramic Detailer, etc., as frequently as you'd like. The only thing to caution about is using waxes on your coating (Gyeon Wax is fine) because most waxes have strong solvents that may affect the coating.

I have a 'high-spot', what do I do?
High spots refer to dried coatings that were not completely buffed off. If you catch the high spots within 30 minutes, you can use the coating itself again to level/soften the high spots. If it's been a few days, then you'll need to mechanically polish it off or use Gyeon Total Remover to remove and reapply coating on the affected area.

What can I wash it with afterwards?
Any pH-neutral soap is suitable for use, and Gyeon recommends Bathe and Bathe+. Ideally, avoid using wash and 'wax' products. While you can use them, it's worth noting that a wash and 'wax' product tends to diminish the water-beading properties of your coating. This results in reduced hydrophobicity after washing. After all, who would want that?!

What's the expiration date? New and opened.
Officially, Gyeon recommends the product to be used within 2 to 3 years when new. If the bottle has been opened, it's best to use up the product in 1 to 2 months to preserve the coating's maximum effectiveness.

Can I apply it on PPF, Trim, Plastics, Wheels, Chrome and Windows?
The short answer is Yes.
PPF: Since the material is more porous and grabbier, you'll need to wipe off the coating at a faster rate. It's best to use Gyeon PPF Coating.
Trim & Plastics: Yes, though it will not darken and 'restore' like Gyeon Trim does.
Wheels, Chrome & Metal: Yes. You can also consider Gyeon's more cost-effective alternative for wheels, Gyeon Rim.
Windows: Technically yes, but avoid the front windshield, as certain wiper/washer fluid combos may chatter. Use Gyeon View or QuickView for chatter-free experience.

Can it be shipped in the cold?
No problem at all. Coatings contain a significant amount of solvents and exhibit high chemical stability.

Is this really the best ceramic coating out there?
Indeed, though there are many coatings on the market, Mohs EVO is something we would personally apply to our own vehicles. It's very slick, durable, and easy to apply (though you've probably heard everyone make these claims). What really stood out for us was its durability. Weather doesn't get as tough as in Calgary, making it the perfect testing ground for us to see what really works, and Mohs EVO has passed the torture on our daily vehicles (that parked outdoors).
We think what contributes to the coating's durability is its slickness, the ability to shed off road salts and other contaminants at a faster rate, not letting it dwell on the paint for too long, thus preventing degradation.
Now, with Skin EVO, it mimics the candy apple look of Gyeon Pure EVO. If you're considering trying a ceramic coating, Syncro is the one to go for.

Product Description

The Gyeon Syncro Evo is a unique coating system designed to provide long-lasting performance, protection and self-cleaning properties! Most coating manufacturers offer coatings and other separate products you can use as a topper to enhance hydrophobic properties, add some gloss, and help keep the coating layer protected and performing it's best. With the original Syncro, Gyeon came up with an easy to use, two step coating process that includes everything from application materials, to the coating, to the topper. With Syncro Evo, you will have everything you loved about Syncro, but enhanced for increased durability, gloss, and easier application. After thoroughly cleaning, polishing and prepping your paint, you will want to apply the included Mohs Evo, followed by Skin Evo and finally topped with the Cure. This three step, 3-4 layer application will greatly enhance gloss and leave you with a durable layer of protection for up to 50 months. Future cleanings will be much easier as less contamination will stick to the paint and for the dirt and grime that does, it will be easier to remove during your wash process.

Gyeon coatings have been completely redesigned and this technology has never used before in car coatings. Evo products utilize a world-first use of the fluoro-modified polisylazane technology that pushes the Evo line to the forefront of car coatings. This technology means extended durability, extreme chemical resistance, longer lasting performance, and only one layer is needed. It remains easy to apply and much easier wipe off than before.

If you want to step up your coating game, give the Gyeon Syncro Evo a try!

• Yüzeyin toz, su lekesi ve parlatıcı artıklarından arındığından emin olun.
2.	Hazırlık & Damlatma
• Coating Applicator Mini bloğunu Q²M Suede ile sarın.
• Pipete 6–8 damla Q² One EVO damlatın (her panel için).
• Kapağın sıkı kapalı, pipetin temiz ve kuru olduğuna dikkat edin.
3.	Çapraz Serpme (Panel Bazlı)
• Omuz genişliği (50×50 cm) alan seçin.
• Önce dikey, sonra yatay geçişlerle ince, homojen bir film oluşturun.
• Yüzey hâlâ ıslak ve eşit dağılmışsa uygulama tamamdır.
4.	Terleme Takibi
• 30–120 sn içinde yüzey “terleyip” ince küçük boncuklar oluşturur.
• Işık altında hafif sis (hafifıslak parlaklık) görünce silme vaktidir.
5.	Silme & Parlatma
• 1. Bez: Q²M BaldWipe ile nazikçe, dairesel hareketlerle kalıntıları alın.
• 2. Bez: Q²M SoftWipe ile tek yönlü silerek candy gloss’u ortaya çıkarın.
• Spot ışık ile paneli kontrol edin; iz veya leke varsa anında düzeltin.
6.	Kürleşme
• Aracı en az 12 saat kuru, tozsuz ve gölgeli bir ortamda bekletin.
• İlk 7 gün deterjan kullanmayın; isteğe bağlı IR lamba (60 °C × 10 dk) süreci hızlandırır.
7.	İkinci Kat (Opsiyonel)
• İlk katın üzerinden ? 60 dk sonra aynı adımlarla ince kat uygulayın.
• İkinci kat, ekstra hidrofobi ve parlaklık sağlar.
8.	İlk Bakım & Koruma
• Uygulamadan 1 saat sonra Q²M Cure ile üst katmanı güçlendirin.
• Rutin yıkamalarda Q²M CeramicDetailer veya Q²M WetCoat ile performansı tazeleyin.

C: 12 saat sonra su ve toz temasına açıktır; tam sertleşme 14 gün sürer.

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Aracı yıkayın; gerekirse kil ve polisaj ile kontaminantları giderin.

6. Araç 12 saat kuru, tozsuz ortamda beklesin; ilk 7 gün deterjan kullanmayın.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Araç boyasında UV koruması, kimyasal direnç ve kolay temizlenebilirlik için tek kat seramik kaplama olarak kullanılır.

### Hedef Yüzeyler
Otomotiv tüm boyalı yüzeyler, motosiklet ve bisiklet çerçeveleri, cam ve parlak plastik aksesuarlar

### Neden Bu Ürün?
• 24 ay / 25.000 km dayanım
• pH 2-11 kimyasal direnç
• 9H sertlik - mikro çiziklere karşı koruma
• 100 ml ile 4 araç kaplama

### Sıkça Sorulan Sorular

C: Evet, ikinci kat için min. 1 saat bekleyip ince tabaka sürün.

**S: Soğuk havada uygulama yapılır mı?**
C: 5°C altı önerilmez; ılık ortamda en iyi sonucu verir.

**S: İlk yıkamadan ne kadar süre sonra araç trafiğe çıkar?**
C: 12 saat sonra su ve toz temasına açıktır; tam sertleşme 14 gün sürer.

> Hidrofobi Takviyesi — Kaplama ömrünü uzatır, 6 hafta koruma ekler.
